function killFrames() {
if (top.location != location) {
if (document.referrer) {
var referrerHostname = get_hostname_from_url(document.referrer);
var strLength = referrerHostname.length;
if ((strLength == 11) && (referrerHostname != "walmart.com")){  // to take care of http://walmart.com url - length of "walmart.com" string is 11.
top.location.replace(document.location.href);
} else if (strLength != 11 && referrerHostname.substring(referrerHostname.length - 12) != ".walmart.com") {  // length og ".walmart.com" string is 12.
top.location.replace(document.location.href);
}
}
}
if (top.frames.length!=0)
top.location=self.document.location;
};
function get_hostname_from_url(url) {
return url.match(/:\/\/(.[^/?]+)/)[1];
};
killFrames();
</script>

var g0041s6HasSearchQuery;
function g0041s6SetSearchQuery(hasSearchQuery, search_queryValue) {
var search_query = document.searchbox.search_query;
if (hasSearchQuery) {
g0041s6HasSearchQuery = true;
search_query.value = search_queryValue;
search_query.style.color = "#333333";
}
else {
g0041s6HasSearchQuery = false;
search_query.value = "Search";
search_query.style.color = "#999999";
}
}
g0041s6SetSearchQuery(WALMART.page.search_query, WALMART.page.search_query);
WALMART.page.g0041s6 = {
validate: function () {
if (!g0041s6HasSearchQuery) {
document.searchbox.search_query.value = "";
}
return true;
}
, focus: function () {
if (!g0041s6HasSearchQuery) {
g0041s6SetSearchQuery(true, "");
}
}
, blur: function () {
if (document.searchbox.search_query.value.length == 0) {
g0041s6SetSearchQuery(false);
}
}
, submit: function () {
return WALMART.page.g0041s6.validate() && document.searchbox.submit();
}
, set: function (value) {
g0041s6SetSearchQuery(value, value);
}
}

var _getOverlayUrl = function (input) {
var url = '/storeLocator/storeFinderNew.do?serviceName=ALL&sfatt=ALL';
if (typeof input != "undefined" && input != null) {
url += '&sfsearch_single_line_address=' + escape(input) + '&sfradius=50';
} else if (WALMART.storeFinder.overlay.isPreferredStoreSetInCookie()) {
url += '&sfsearch_single_line_address=' + WALMART.storeFinder.overlay.getZipCodeFromCookie() + '&sfradius=50';
}
return url;
};
function openStoreFinderOverlay(input) {
WALMART.storeFinder.overlay.open(input, 'Select Your Store', _getOverlayUrl);
}</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
function doLink(target, catNavId, type) {
var querySeparator = "&";
if (target.indexOf("?") == -1) {
querySeparator = "?";
}
if (type == 'E') {
document.location = target;
} else {
if (target.indexOf('catNavId') != -1 || catNavId == null || catNavId == undefined) {
document.location = target + querySeparator + "fromPageCatId=" + 91848;
} else {
document.location = target + querySeparator + "fromPageCatId=" + 91848 + "&catNavId=" + catNavId;
}
}
}
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
function getRVIdata(commaSeparatedItemList){
var itemList = commaSeparatedItemList.split(',');
WALMART.recentlyvieweditems.contentHost = 'content-cdn.walmart.com';
if (typeof WALMART.recentlyvieweditems.contentHost == 'undefined') {
WALMART.recentlyvieweditems.contentHost = '';
}
WALMART.recentlyvieweditems.counter = itemList.length;
for (var item in itemList) {
WALMART.recentlyvieweditems.AjaxObject_RecentlyViewed.startRequest(itemList[item]);
}
}
(function ($, undefined) {
var rvi = WALMART.recentlyvieweditems
, RVI = rvi.RecentlyViewedItems
;
rvi.display = "";
rvi.contentHost = "content-cdn.walmart.com";
RVI.imageHost = "http://i2.walmartimages.com";
RVI.itemId = "";
rvi.listOfItems = RVI.getRecentlyViewedItemsList();
rvi.show
= RVI.areRecentlyViewedItemsSetInCookie("false")
? function () {
if (rvi.display == "") {
//start AJAX call:
getRVIdata(RVI.getRVItemsList('false'));
$("#rvi").css("display", rvi.display);
$("#rviClear").click(function () {
RVI.updatePersistentCookie("false", "");
$("#rvi_none").css("display", "");
$("#rvi").css("display", "none");
});
}
}
: function() {
if (rvi.display == "") {
$("#rvi_none").css("display", rvi.display);
}
};
$(window).load( function () {
$("#rvi_wrapper").viewed(rvi.show);
}
);
})(WALMART.jQuery);
</script>

<div id="detailedPageDescriptionCopyBlock">
<a name="462842"></a>
<b>Entertainment Centers</b><p>
Entertainment centers. Entertainment centers and TV consoles cost less at Walmart. Save on a new entertainment center to dramatically enhance your viewing and listening experience, as well as the overall look and feel of your living room. We have entertainment centers and TV consoles to choose from in all shapes, sizes and shades, so you're certain to find the entertainment center or TV console you want while saving money. <p>
What sort of entertainment center or TV console are you looking for? We have oak entertainment centers, metal entertainment centers, black TV consoles, white TV stands and just about every other type of entertainment center or TV console you can imagine. Best of all, our Every Day Low Prices make it easy to save on TV furniture like entertainment centers and TV consoles. <p>
You'll find more here in the way of furniture than simply entertainment centers, of course. In addition to our broad TV console, TV stand and entertainment center selection, you'll save on household necessities like <a href="http://www.walmart.com/cp/4038">living room furniture</a>, <a href="http://www.walmart.com/cp/office-furniture/97116">home office furniture</a>, <a href="http://www.walmart.com/cp/4037">kitchen and dining room furniture</a>, to mention just a small assortment of the furniture items we carry. <p>
Upgrade your living room today with a new entertainment center or TV console at terrific low price from Walmart. Now <i>that's</i> entertainment! <p>
</div>
